placeholder=\u0026quot;Start typing...\u0026quot;\n      editor={editor}\n      plugins={[ReactListPlugin, ReactLinkPlugin, ReactImagePlugin, ReactCodeblockPlugin]}\n      slashOption={{\n ReactLinkPlugin\n│   │   │   ├── command/        # Link commands\n│   │   │   └── utils/          # URL validation and detection\n│   │   │\n│   │   ├── list/               # 📋 Lists (ordered/unordered)\n│   │   │   ├── plugin/         # List plugin with nesting\n│   │   │   ├── react/          # ReactListPlugin\n│   │   │   ├── command/        # List manipulation commands\n│   │   │   └── utils/          # List operations\n│   │   │\n│   │   └── hr/                 # ➖ Horizontal rules\n│   │       ├── plugin/         # HR plugin with styling\n│   │       ├── react/          # ReactHRPlugin\n│   │       ├── command/        # HR insertion commands\n│   │       └── node/           # HorizontalRuleNode\n│   │\n│   ├── react/                  # ⚛️ High-level React components\n│   │   ├── Editor/             # Main Editor component with plugins\n│   │   ├── ChatInput/          # Chat interface component\n│   │   ├── ChatInputActions/   # Chat action buttons\n│   │   ├── ChatInputActionBar/ # Action bar layout\n│   │   ├── SendButton/         # Send button with states\n│   │   └── CodeLanguageSelect/ # Code language selector\n│   │\n│   └── index.ts                # Public API exports\n│\n├── docs/                       # 📚 Documentation source\n├── tests/                      # 🧪 Test files\n├── vitest.config.ts           # Test configuration\n└── .dumi/                      # Dumi doc build cache\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe architecture follows a \u003cstrong\u003edual-layer design\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKernel Layer\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003eeditor-kernel/\u003c/code\u003e) - Framework-agnostic core with plugin system\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReact Layer\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003ereact/\u003c/code\u003e + \u003ccode\u003eplugins/*/react/\u003c/code\u003e) - React-specific implementations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEach plugin follows a consistent structure:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003eplugin/\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e - Core plugin logic and node definitions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003ereact/\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e - React components and hooks (if applicable)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecommand/\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e - Editor commands and handlers\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003eservice/\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e - Services and business logic\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003enode/\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e - Custom Lexical nodes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003eutils/\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e - Utility functions and helpers\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis allows for maximum flexibility - you can use just the kernel for custom integrations, or the React components for rapid development.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv align=\"right\" <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">LobeHub Editor</h1><a id="user-content-lobehub-editor" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: LobeHub Editor" href="#lobehub-editor"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A modern, extensible rich text editor built on Meta's Lexical framework with dual-architecture design, featuring both a powerful kernel and React integration. Optimized for AI applications and chat interfaces.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/@lobehub/editor" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/00143d6d8bb10f88a16ec640add58e20c289761d256df9ba491ee54ae388026b/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f762f406c6f62656875622f656469746f723f636f6c6f723d333639656666266c6162656c436f6c6f723d626c61636b266c6f676f3d6e706d266c6f676f436f6c6f723d7768697465267374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/v/@lobehub/editor?color=369eff&amp;labelColor=black&amp;logo=npm&amp;logoColor=white&amp;style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">✨ Features</h2><a id="user-content--features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ✨ Features" href="#-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🎯 <strong>Dual Architecture</strong> - Both kernel-based API and React components for maximum flexibility</li>
<li>⚛️ <strong>React-First</strong> - Built for React 19+ with modern hooks and patterns</li>
<li>🔌 <strong>Rich Plugin Ecosystem</strong> - 10+ built-in plugins for comprehensive content editing</li>
<li>💬 <strong>Chat Interface Ready</strong> - Pre-built chat input components with mention support</li>
<li>⌨️ <strong>Slash Commands</strong> - Intuitive <code>/</code> and <code>@</code> triggered menus for quick content insertion</li>
<li>📝 <strong>Multiple Export Formats</strong> - JSON, Markdown, and plain text export capabilities</li>
<li>🎨 <strong>Customizable UI</strong> - Antd-styled components with flexible theming</li>
<li>🔗 <strong>File &amp; Media Support</strong> - Native support for images, files, tables, and more</li>
<li>🎯 <strong>TypeScript Native</strong> - Built with TypeScript for excellent developer experience</li>
<li>📱 <strong>Modern Build System</strong> - Optimized with Vite, Dumi docs, and comprehensive testing</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📦 Installation</h2><a id="user-content--installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📦 Installation" href="#-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To install <code>@lobehub/editor</code>, run the following command:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://bun.sh" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/25f28e161904a25aead369b2968902f04daebafbc1b207c6def144fb7ae4d8ae/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d737065656475702532307769746825323062756e2d626c61636b3f6c6f676f3d62756e267374796c653d666f722d7468652d6261646765" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-speedup%20with%20bun-black?logo=bun&amp;style=for-the-badge" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ bun add @lobehub/editor"><pre>$ bun add @lobehub/editor</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ pnpm add @lobehub/editor"><pre>$ pnpm add @lobehub/editor</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🚀 Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content--quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🚀 Quick Start" href="#-quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Basic Editor</h3><a id="user-content-basic-editor" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Basic Editor" href="#basic-editor"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The simplest way to get started with a fully-featured editor:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-tsx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  INSERT_HEADING_COMMAND,
  ReactCodeblockPlugin,
  ReactImagePlugin,
  ReactLinkPlugin,
  ReactListPlugin,
} from '@lobehub/editor';
import { Editor, useEditor } from '@lobehub/editor/react';

export default function MyEditor() {
  const editor = useEditor();

  return (
    &lt;Editor
      placeholder=&quot;Start typing...&quot;
      editor={editor}
      plugins={[ReactListPlugin, ReactLinkPlugin, ReactImagePlugin, ReactCodeblockPlugin]}
      slashOption={{
        items: [
          {
            key: 'h1',
            label: 'Heading 1',
            onSelect: (editor) =&gt; {
              editor.dispatchCommand(INSERT_HEADING_COMMAND, { tag: 'h1' });
            },
          },
          // More slash commands...
        ],
      }}
      onChange={(editor) =&gt; {
        // Handle content changes
        const markdown = editor.getDocument('markdown');
        const json = editor.getDocument('json');
      }}
    /&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">MyEditor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

          <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Advanced Usage with Plugins</h3><a id="user-content-advanced-usage-with-plugins" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Advanced Usage with Plugins" href="#advanced-usage-with-plugins"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Add more functionality with built-in plugins:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-tsx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  INSERT_FILE_COMMAND,
  INSERT_MENTION_COMMAND,
  INSERT_TABLE_COMMAND,
  ReactFilePlugin,
  ReactHRPlugin,
  ReactTablePlugin,
} from '@lobehub/editor';
import { Editor, useEditor } from '@lobehub/editor/react';

export default function AdvancedEditor() {
  const editor = useEditor();

  return (
    &lt;Editor
      editor={editor}
      plugins={[
        ReactTablePlugin,
        ReactHRPlugin,
        Editor.withProps(ReactFilePlugin, {
          handleUpload: async (file) =&gt; {
            // Handle file upload
            return { url: await uploadFile(file) };
          },
        }),
      ]}
      mentionOption={{
        items: async (search) =&gt; [
          {
            key: 'user1',
            label: 'John Doe',
            onSelect: (editor) =&gt; {
              editor.dispatchCommand(INSERT_MENTION_COMMAND, {
                label: 'John Doe',
                extra: { userId: 1 },
              });
            },
          },
        ],
      }}
    /&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Chat Input Component</h3><a id="user-content-chat-input-component" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Chat Input Component" href="#chat-input-component"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Pre-built component optimized for chat interfaces:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-tsx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { ChatInput } from '@lobehub/editor/react';

  );

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Editor Kernel API</h3><a id="user-content-editor-kernel-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Editor Kernel API" href="#editor-kernel-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For advanced use cases, access the underlying kernel directly:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { IEditor, createEditor } from '@lobehub/editor';

// Create editor instance
const editor: IEditor = createEditor();

// Register plugins
editor.registerPlugin(SomePlugin, { config: 'value' });

// Interact with content
editor.setDocument('text', 'Hello world');
const content = editor.getDocument('json');

// Listen to events
editor.on('content-changed', (newContent) =&gt; {
  console.log('Content updated:', newContent);
});

// Execute commands
editor.dispatchCommand(INSERT_HEADING_COMMAND, { tag: 'h2' });"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">IEditor</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">createEditor</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'@lobehub/editor'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Create editor instance</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">editor</span>: <span class="pl-smi">IEditor</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createEditor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Register plugins</span>
<span class="pl-s1">editor</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerPlugin</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">SomePlugin</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">config</span>: <span class="pl-s">'value'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Interact with content</span>
<span class="pl-s1">editor</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setDocument</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'text'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'Hello world'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">content</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">editor</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getDocument</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'json'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Listen to events</span>
<span class="pl-s1">editor</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'content-changed'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">newContent</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Content updated:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">newContent</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Execute commands</span>
<span class="pl-s1">editor</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">dispatchCommand</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">INSERT_HEADING_COMMAND</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">tag</span>: <span class="pl-s">'h2'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div align="right" dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">[![]<a href="#readme-top">back-to-top]</a></p>
</div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Plugin Architecture</h3><a id="user-content-plugin-architecture" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Plugin Architecture" href="#plugin-architecture"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All plugins follow a <strong>dual-architecture design</strong>:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🧠 <strong>Kernel Layer</strong> (Framework-agnostic)</h4><a id="user-content--kernel-layer-framework-agnostic" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🧠 Kernel Layer (Framework-agnostic)" href="#-kernel-layer-framework-agnostic"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Plugin Interface</strong>: Standardized plugin system with lifecycle management</li>
<li><strong>Service Container</strong>: Centralized service registration and dependency injection</li>
<li><strong>Command System</strong>: Event-driven command pattern for editor operations</li>
<li><strong>Node System</strong>: Custom node types with serialization and transformation</li>
<li><strong>Data Sources</strong>: Content management and format conversion (JSON, Markdown, Text)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">⚛️ <strong>React Layer</strong> (React-specific)</h4><a id="user-content-️-react-layer-react-specific" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ⚛️ React Layer (React-specific)" href="#️-react-layer-react-specific"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>React Components</strong>: High-level components for easy integration</li>
<li><strong>Hook Integration</strong>: Custom hooks for editor state and functionality</li>
<li><strong>Event Handling</strong>: React-friendly event system and callbacks</li>
<li><strong>UI Components</strong>: Pre-built UI elements with theming support</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Plugin Features</h3><a id="user-content-plugin-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Plugin Features" href="#plugin-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>Fully configurable</strong> with TypeScript-typed options</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Composable</strong> - use any combination together</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Extensible</strong> - create custom plugins using the same API</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Event-driven</strong> - react to user interactions and content changes</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Service-oriented</strong> - modular architecture with dependency injection</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Internationalization</strong> - Built-in i18n support where applicable</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Markdown integration</strong> - Shortcuts, import/export, custom transformers</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Theme system</strong> - Customizable styling and appearance</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Command pattern</strong> - Programmatic control and automation</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📖 API Reference</h2><a id="user-content--api-reference" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📖 API Reference" href="#-api-reference"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Utility Hooks</h4><a id="user-content-utility-hooks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Utility Hooks" href="#utility-hooks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-tsx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Get editor instance
const editor = useEditor();

// Helper for plugin configuration
const PluginWithConfig = Editor.withProps(ReactFilePlugin, {
  handleUpload: async (file) =&gt; ({ url: 'uploaded-url' }),
});"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Get editor instance</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">PluginWithConfig</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Editor</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">withProps</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">ReactFilePlugin</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Editor Kernel</h3><a id="user-content-editor-kernel" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Editor Kernel" href="#editor-kernel"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>createEditor(): IEditor</code></h4><a id="user-content-createeditor-ieditor" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: createEditor(): IEditor" href="#createeditor-ieditor"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a new editor kernel instance:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const editor = createEditor();"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">editor</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createEditor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>IEditor</code> Interface</h4><a id="user-content-ieditor-interface" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: IEditor Interface" href="#ieditor-interface"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Core editor methods:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="interface IEditor {
  // Content management
  setDocument(type: string, content: any): void;
  getDocument(type: string): any;

  // Plugin system
  registerPlugin&lt;T&gt;(plugin: Constructor&lt;T&gt;, config?: T): IEditor;
  registerPlugins(plugins: Plugin[]): IEditor;

  // Commands
  dispatchCommand&lt;T&gt;(command: LexicalCommand&lt;T&gt;, payload: T): boolean;

  // Events
  on&lt;T&gt;(event: string, listener: (data: T) =&gt; void): this;
  off&lt;T&gt;(event: string, listener: (data: T) =&gt; void): this;

  // Lifecycle
  focus(): void;
  blur(): void;
  destroy(): void;

  // Access
  getLexicalEditor(): LexicalEditor | null;
  getRootElement(): HTMLElement | null;
  requireService&lt;T&gt;(serviceId: ServiceID&lt;T&gt;): T | null;
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">interface</span> <span class="pl-smi">IEditor</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Content management</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">setDocument</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">type</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">content</span>: <span class="pl-smi">any</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi"><span class="pl-k">void</span></span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">getDocument</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">type</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi">any</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// Plugin system</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">registerPlugin</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">plugin</span>: <span class="pl-smi">Constructor</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span>?: <span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi">IEditor</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">registerPlugins</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">plugins</span>: <span class="pl-smi">Plugin</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi">IEditor</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// Commands</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">dispatchCommand</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">command</span>: <span class="pl-smi">LexicalCommand</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">payload</span>: <span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi">boolean</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// Events</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">on</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">event</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">listener</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">data</span>: <span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi"><span class="pl-k">void</span></span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: this<span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">off</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">event</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">listener</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">data</span>: <span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi"><span class="pl-k">void</span></span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: this<span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// Lifecycle</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">focus</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi"><span class="pl-k">void</span></span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">blur</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi"><span class="pl-k">void</span></span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">destroy</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi"><span class="pl-k">void</span></span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// Access</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">getLexicalEditor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi">LexicalEditor</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">getRootElement</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi">HTMLElement</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">requireService</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">serviceId</span>: <span class="pl-smi">ServiceID</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">T</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>: <span class="pl-smi">T</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Plugin System</h3><a id="user-content-plugin-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Plugin System" href="#plugin-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Creating Custom Plugins</h4><a id="user-content-creating-custom-plugins" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Creating Custom Plugins" href="#creating-custom-plugins"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { IEditorKernel, IEditorPlugin } from '@lobehub/editor';

class MyCustomPlugin implements IEditorPlugin {
  constructor(private config: MyPluginConfig) {}

  initialize(kernel: IEditorKernel) {
    // Register nodes, commands, transforms, etc.
    kernel.registerNode(MyCustomNode);
    kernel.registerCommand(MY_COMMAND, this.handleCommand);
  }

  destroy() {
    // Cleanup
  }
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">IEditorKernel</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">IEditorPlugin</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'@lobehub/editor'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-smi">MyCustomPlugin</span> <span class="pl-k">implements</span> <span class="pl-smi">IEditorPlugin</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span>: <span class="pl-smi">MyPluginConfig</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">initialize</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">kernel</span>: <span class="pl-smi">IEditorKernel</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Register nodes, commands, transforms, etc.</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">kernel</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerNode</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">MyCustomNode</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">kernel</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerCommand</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">MY_COMMAND</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">handleCommand</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">destroy</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Cleanup</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Available Commands</h4><a id="user-content-available-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Available Commands" href="#available-commands"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Common commands you can dispatch:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Content insertion
INSERT_HEADING_COMMAND; // { tag: 'h1' | 'h2' | 'h3' }
INSERT_LINK_COMMAND; // { url: string, text?: string }
INSERT_IMAGE_COMMAND; // { src: string, alt?: string }
INSERT_TABLE_COMMAND; // { rows: number, columns: number }
INSERT_MENTION_COMMAND; // { label: string, extra?: any }
INSERT_FILE_COMMAND; // { file: File }
INSERT_HORIZONTAL_RULE_COMMAND;

// Text formatting
FORMAT_TEXT_COMMAND; // { format: 'bold' | 'italic' | 'underline' }
CLEAR_FORMAT_COMMAND;"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Content insertion</span>
<span class="pl-c1">INSERT_HEADING_COMMAND</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// { tag: 'h1' | 'h2' | 'h3' }</span>
<span class="pl-c1">INSERT_LINK_COMMAND</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// { url: string, text?: string }</span>
<span class="pl-c1">INSERT_IMAGE_COMMAND</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// { src: string, alt?: string }</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Text formatting</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Setup</h3><a id="user-content-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Setup" href="#setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can use Github Codespaces for online development:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://codespaces.new/lobehub/lobe-editor" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://github.com/codespaces/badge.svg" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Or clone it for local development:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://bun.sh" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/25f28e161904a25aead369b2968902f04daebafbc1b207c6def144fb7ae4d8ae/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d737065656475702532307769746825323062756e2d626c61636b3f6c6f676f3d62756e267374796c653d666f722d7468652d6261646765" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-speedup%20with%20bun-black?logo=bun&amp;style=for-the-badge" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ git clone https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-editor.git
$ cd lobe-editor
$ pnpm install
$ pnpm run dev"><pre>$ git clone https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-editor.git
$ <span class="pl-c1">cd</span> lobe-editor
$ pnpm install
$ pnpm run dev</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This will start the Dumi documentation server with live playground at <code>http://localhost:8000</code>.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Debug Environment Variables</h3><a id="user-content-debug-environment-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Debug Environment Variables" href="#debug-environment-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">LobeHub Editor includes comprehensive debug logging that can be controlled via environment variables:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Basic Debug Configuration</h4><a id="user-content-basic-debug-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Basic Debug Configuration" href="#basic-debug-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Enable all LobeHub Editor debug output
DEBUG=lobe-editor:*

# Enable only important logs (recommended for development)
DEBUG=lobe-editor:*:info,lobe-editor:*:warn,lobe-editor:*:error

# Enable specific components
DEBUG=lobe-editor:kernel,lobe-editor:plugin:*"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Enable all LobeHub Editor debug output</span>
DEBUG=lobe-editor:<span class="pl-k">*</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Enable only important logs (recommended for development)</span>
DEBUG=lobe-editor:<span class="pl-k">*</span>:info,lobe-editor:<span class="pl-k">*</span>:warn,lobe-editor:<span class="pl-k">*</span>:error

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Enable specific components</span>
DEBUG=lobe-editor:kernel,lobe-editor:plugin:<span class="pl-k">*</span></pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Development Usage</h4><a id="user-content-development-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Development Usage" href="#development-usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

# Only critical logs

# Plugin debugging
DEBUG=lobe-editor:plugin:*
# Service debugging

<p dir="auto">The architecture follows a <strong>dual-layer design</strong>:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Kernel Layer</strong> (<code>editor-kernel/</code>) - Framework-agnostic core with plugin system</li>
<li><strong>React Layer</strong> (<code>react/</code> + <code>plugins/*/react/</code>) - React-specific implementations</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Each plugin follows a consistent structure:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>plugin/</code></strong> - Core plugin logic and node definitions</li>
<li><strong><code>react/</code></strong> - React components and hooks (if applicable)</li>
<li><strong><code>command/</code></strong> - Editor commands and handlers</li>
<li><strong><code>service/</code></strong> - Services and business logic</li>
<li><strong><code>node/</code></strong> - Custom Lexical nodes</li>
<li><strong><code>utils/</code></strong> - Utility functions and helpers</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">This allows for maximum flexibility - you can use just the kernel for custom integrations, or the React components for rapid development.</p>
<div align="right" dir="auto">
<p dir="auto"><a href="#readme-top"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/290fbed7daf3fc5c7b5a66242bf583afb557e012eec8eed267369cd80d2be31a/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2d4241434b5f544f5f544f502d626c61636b3f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/-BACK_TO_TOP-black?style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🤝 Contributing</h2><a id="user-content--contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🤝 Contributing" href="#-contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Contributions of all types are more than welcome, if you are interested in contributing code, feel free to check out our GitHub <a href="https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-editor/issues">Issues</a> to get stuck in to show us what you're made of.</p>

        ✒️ Lobe Editor - a modern, extensible rich text editor built on Meta's Lexical framework with dual-architecture design, featuring both a powerful kernel and React integration. Optimized for AI applications and chat interfaces.
      </p>
